[x*(c+a^2*c*x^2)/arctan(a*x)^2,x,0,Unintegrable(x*(c+a^2*c*x^2)/arctan(a*x)^2,x)],
[(c+a^2*c*x^2)/arctan(a*x)^2,x,0,Unintegrable((c+a^2*c*x^2)/arctan(a*x)^2,x)],
[(c+a^2*c*x^2)/(x*arctan(a*x)^2),x,0,Unintegrable((c+a^2*c*x^2)/(x*arctan(a*x)^2),x)],
[x*(c+a^2*c*x^2)^2/arctan(a*x)^2,x,0,Unintegrable(x*(c+a^2*c*x^2)^2/arctan(a*x)^2,x)],
[(c+a^2*c*x^2)^2/arctan(a*x)^2,x,0,Unintegrable((c+a^2*c*x^2)^2/arctan(a*x)^2,x)],
[(c+a^2*c*x^2)^2/(x*arctan(a*x)^2),x,0,Unintegrable((c+a^2*c*x^2)^2/(x*arctan(a*x)^2),x)],
[x*(c+a^2*c*x^2)^3/arctan(a*x)^2,x,0,Unintegrable(x*(c+a^2*c*x^2)^3/arctan(a*x)^2,x)],
[(c+a^2*c*x^2)^3/arctan(a*x)^2,x,0,Unintegrable((c+a^2*c*x^2)^3/arctan(a*x)^2,x)],
[(c+a^2*c*x^2)^3/(x*arctan(a*x)^2),x,0,Unintegrable((c+a^2*c*x^2)^3/(x*arctan(a*x)^2),x)],

# q<0
[x^3/((c+a^2*c*x^2)*arctan(a*x)^2),x,1,-x^3/(a*c*arctan(a*x))+3*Unintegrable(x^2/arctan(a*x),x)/(a*c)],
[x^2/((c+a^2*c*x^2)*arctan(a*x)^2),x,1,-x^2/(a*c*arctan(a*x))+2*Unintegrable(x/arctan(a*x),x)/(a*c)],
[x/((c+a^2*c*x^2)*arctan(a*x)^2),x,1,-x/(a*c*arctan(a*x))+Unintegrable(1/arctan(a*x),x)/(a*c)],
[1/((c+a^2*c*x^2)*arctan(a*x)^2),x,1,(-1)/(a*c*arctan(a*x))],
[1/(x*(c+a^2*c*x^2)*arctan(a*x)^2),x,1,(-1)/(a*c*x*arctan(a*x))-Unintegrable(1/(x^2*arctan(a*x)),x)/(a*c)],
[1/(x^2*(c+a^2*c*x^2)*arctan(a*x)^2),x,1,(-1)/(a*c*x^2*arctan(a*x))-2*Unintegrable(1/(x^3*arctan(a*x)),x)/(a*c)],
[1/(x^3*(c+a^2*c*x^2)*arctan(a*x)^2),x,1,(-1)/(a*c*x^3*arctan(a*x))-3*Unintegrable(1/(x^4*arctan(a*x)),x)/(a*c)],
[1/(x^4*(c+a^2*c*x^2)*arctan(a*x)^2),x,1,(-1)/(a*c*x^4*arctan(a*x))-4*Unintegrable(1/(x^5*arctan(a*x)),x)/(a*c)],
[x^3/((c+a^2*c*x^2)^2*arctan(a*x)^2),x,11,-x/(a^3*c^2*arctan(a*x))+x/(a^3*c^2*(1+a^2*x^2)*arctan(a*x))-Ci(2*arctan(a*x))/(a^4*c^2)+Unintegrable(1/arctan(a*x),x)/(a^3*c^2)],
[x^2/((c+a^2*c*x^2)^2*arctan(a*x)^2),x,5,-x^2/(a*c^2*(1+a^2*x^2)*arctan(a*x))+Si(2*arctan(a*x))/(a^3*c^2)],
[x/((c+a^2*c*x^2)^2*arctan(a*x)^2),x,9,-x/(a*c^2*(1+a^2*x^2)*arctan(a*x))+Ci(2*arctan(a*x))/(a^2*c^2)],
[1/((c+a^2*c*x^2)^2*arctan(a*x)^2),x,5,(-1)/(a*c^2*(1+a^2*x^2)*arctan(a*x))-Si(2*arctan(a*x))/(a*c^2)],
[1/(x*(c+a^2*c*x^2)^2*arctan(a*x)^2),x,11,(-1)/(a*c^2*x*arctan(a*x))+a*x/(c^2*(1+a^2*x^2)*arctan(a*x))-Ci(2*arctan(a*x))/c^2-Unintegrable(1/(x^2*arctan(a*x)),x)/(a*c^2)],
[1/(x^2*(c+a^2*c*x^2)^2*arctan(a*x)^2),x,7,(-1)/(a*c^2*x^2*arctan(a*x))+a/(c^2*(1+a^2*x^2)*arctan(a*x))+a*Si(2*arctan(a*x))/c^2-2*Unintegrable(1/(x^3*arctan(a*x)),x)/(a*c^2)],
[1/(x^3*(c+a^2*c*x^2)^2*arctan(a*x)^2),x,13,(-1)/(a*c^2*x^3*arctan(a*x))+a/(c^2*x*arctan(a*x))-a^3*x/(c^2*(1+a^2*x^2)*arctan(a*x))+a^2*Ci(2*arctan(a*x))/c^2-3*Unintegrable(1/(x^4*arctan(a*x)),x)/(a*c^2)+a*Unintegrable(1/(x^2*arctan(a*x)),x)/c^2],
[1/(x^4*(c+a^2*c*x^2)^2*arctan(a*x)^2),x,9,(-1)/(a*c^2*x^4*arctan(a*x))+a/(c^2*x^2*arctan(a*x))-a^3/(c^2*(1+a^2*x^2)*arctan(a*x))-a^3*Si(2*arctan(a*x))/c^2-4*Unintegrable(1/(x^5*arctan(a*x)),x)/(a*c^2)+2*a*Unintegrable(1/(x^3*arctan(a*x)),x)/c^2],
[x^3/((c+a^2*c*x^2)^3*arctan(a*x)^2),x,20,x/(a^3*c^3*(1+a^2*x^2)^2*arctan(a*x))-x/(a^3*c^3*(1+a^2*x^2)*arctan(a*x))+1/2*Ci(2*arctan(a*x))/(a^4*c^3)-1/2*Ci(4*arctan(a*x))/(a^4*c^3)],

[x/((c+a^2*c*x^2)^3*arctan(a*x)^2),x,10,-x/(a*c^3*(1+a^2*x^2)^2*arctan(a*x))+1/2*Ci(2*arctan(a*x))/(a^2*c^3)+1/2*Ci(4*arctan(a*x))/(a^2*c^3)],
[1/((c+a^2*c*x^2)^3*arctan(a*x)^2),x,6,(-1)/(a*c^3*(1+a^2*x^2)^2*arctan(a*x))-Si(2*arctan(a*x))/(a*c^3)-1/2*Si(4*arctan(a*x))/(a*c^3)],
[1/(x*(c+a^2*c*x^2)^3*arctan(a*x)^2),x,22,(-1)/(a*c^3*x*arctan(a*x))+a*x/(c^3*(1+a^2*x^2)^2*arctan(a*x))+a*x/(c^3*(1+a^2*x^2)*arctan(a*x))-3/2*Ci(2*arctan(a*x))/c^3-1/2*Ci(4*arctan(a*x))/c^3-Unintegrable(1/(x^2*arctan(a*x)),x)/(a*c^3)],
[1/(x^2*(c+a^2*c*x^2)^3*arctan(a*x)^2),x,14,(-1)/(a*c^3*x^2*arctan(a*x))+a/(c^3*(1+a^2*x^2)^2*arctan(a*x))+a/(c^3*(1+a^2*x^2)*arctan(a*x))+2*a*Si(2*arctan(a*x))/c^3+1/2*a*Si(4*arctan(a*x))/c^3-2*Unintegrable(1/(x^3*arctan(a*x)),x)/(a*c^3)],
[1/(x^3*(c+a^2*c*x^2)^3*arctan(a*x)^2),x,36,(-1)/(a*c^3*x^3*arctan(a*x))+2*a/(c^3*x*arctan(a*x))-a^3*x/(c^3*(1+a^2*x^2)^2*arctan(a*x))-2*a^3*x/(c^3*(1+a^2*x^2)*arctan(a*x))+5/2*a^2*Ci(2*arctan(a*x))/c^3+1/2*a^2*Ci(4*arctan(a*x))/c^3-3*Unintegrable(1/(x^4*arctan(a*x)),x)/(a*c^3)+2*a*Unintegrable(1/(x^2*arctan(a*x)),x)/c^3],

# Integrands of the form x^m (d+c^2 d x^2)^(q/2) / (a+b ArcTan[c x])^2
